\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
\subsubsection*{template$<$typename Derived$>$\newline
class Eigen\+::\+Sparse\+Map\+Base$<$ Derived, Read\+Only\+Accessors $>$}
Common base class for \doxylink{classEigen_1_1Map}{Map} and \doxylink{classEigen_1_1Ref}{Ref} instance of sparse matrix and vector. 

class \doxylink{classEigen_1_1SparseMapBase}{Sparse\+Map\+Base}
